\Hypertarget{group__USB__Register__Masks_ga8cfb473cdf63dce69fbae3b03e5fa0b9}\index{USB Register Masks@{USB Register Masks}!USB\_USBTRC0\_USBRESMEN@{USB\_USBTRC0\_USBRESMEN}}

\doxysubsubsubsubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{USB\_USBTRC0\_USBRESMEN}{USB\_USBTRC0\_USBRESMEN}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__USB__Register__Masks_ga8cfb473cdf63dce69fbae3b03e5fa0b9} 
\+\#define USB\+\_\+\+USBTRC0\+\_\+\+USBRESMEN(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{x}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

{\bfseries Value:\+}
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{(((uint8\_t)(((uint8\_t)(x))\ <<\ USB\_USBTRC0\_USBRESMEN\_SHIFT))\ \&\ USB\_USBTRC0\_USBRESMEN\_MASK)}

\end{DoxyCode}
USBRESMEN -\/ Asynchronous Resume Interrupt Enable 0b0..USB asynchronous wakeup from suspend mode disabled. 0b1..USB asynchronous wakeup from suspend mode enabled. The asynchronous resume interrupt differs from the synchronous resume interrupt in that it asynchronously detects K-\/state using the unfiltered state of the D+ and D-\/ pins. This interrupt should only be enabled when the Transceiver is suspended. 

Definition at line \doxymbox{\hyperlink{PERI__USB_8h_source_l00865}{865}} of file \doxymbox{\hyperlink{PERI__USB_8h_source}{PERI\+\_\+\+USB.\+h}}.
